### Candidate 1: `A*c0/(A + c1) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*t*exp(c6*t) + c7`

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2: `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*Abs(A*c9)`

- Cannot simultaneously have A, A^(1/3), and A·exp(αt).
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]
